      <p>
       This is a
       <b>
        list of solar eclipses that will occur in the 23rd century
       </b>
       . During the period 2201 to 2300 there will be 248
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse" title="Solar eclipse">
        solar eclipses
       </a>
       of which 92 will be
       <a href="/wiki/Solar_eclipse#Types" title="Solar eclipse">
        partial
       </a>
       , 86 will be annular, 67 will be total, and 3 will be hybrids. The greatest number of eclipses in one year will be five, in 2206, and three months, December 2206, January 2261, and November 2282 will have two eclipses.
       <sup class="reference" id="cite_ref-nasa_catalog_list_1-0">
        <a href="#cite_note-nasa_catalog_list-1">
         [1]
        </a>
       </sup>
      </p>
